Riga, Latvia News recently received from the area of Dagda (near the Polish border) states that 20 Polish aircraft flew into Latvian territory this morning and landed. Local officials immediately detained them. In addition, a large number of Polish refugees have fled into Lithuanian territory. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Cernăuți, Romania The border between Romania and Poland has recently been sealed off by the Romanian authorities, and trenches have been dug within three kilometers of the border. Civilians are not allowed to travel within seven kilometers of the border without special permission. (Havas on the 18th)

London According to a message transmitted by the German News Agency, Polish President Mościcki led government personnel across the Romanian border in Kutty. According to a French message from Cernăuți on the Polish border, 55 Polish aircraft have landed there. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Cernăuți, Romania Polish President Mościcki has recently arrived at the border town of Kutty with his cabinet members. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Cernăuți, Romania Fifty-five Polish aircraft were chased by German aircraft at noon today and flew into Romanian airspace, landing in Ruyeni, 18 miles from the border. The aircraft and pilots were detained. No Polish government officials came with them, but it is rumored that the Polish Ministry of Foreign Affairs has moved to Romanian territory. In addition, after Soviet troops entered Poland, German aircraft bombed Polish cities near the Romanian border more and more severely. Diplomats from various countries have successively taken refuge in Romania. British Ambassador Sir Reginald Hoare has arrived here, and French Ambassador Noël will arrive here soon. The Romanian government has asked diplomats from various countries to leave this city. In addition, Polish Foreign Minister Colonel Beck will also come here tonight and plans to make an important statement to reporters from various countries. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

London It is difficult to know for sure where the Polish government has moved to at present. People here generally believe that it is often near the border with Romania. However, according to responsible British officials, if the Polish government moves into Romanian territory, it will cause a difficult situation. According to international law, once a government moves into the territory of a neutral country, it cannot continue to exercise its functions. If the Romanian government does not deal with it in accordance with international law, then Germany will inevitably accuse the Romanian government of "hostile attitude" and take action against Romania. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Danzig According to a telegraph from Riga received from Berlin, General Sosnkowski, an old friend of Polish Marshal Piłsudski, attempted to establish a military dictatorship in Warsaw yesterday, but was thwarted by Polish Commander-in-Chief General Rydz-Śmigły. At present, the Polish government has fled, and the headquarters has fallen into complete chaos. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

London British Ambassador to Poland Sir Reginald Hoare followed the advice of the Polish government and led the remaining personnel of the embassy into Romania yesterday. It is heard that the Polish government has moved to Romanian territory or will move there. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Riga Today, this place received a dispatch from Daugavpils, stating that Polish refugees have now begun to flee to the Latvian border. It is heard that 20 Polish aircraft have landed there. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Bucharest After Polish government officials and President Mościcki took refuge in Chernovtsy, Romania, the Romanian government asked them to leave the town and come to Bucharest by special train at noon today. It is heard that diplomatic representatives of various countries to Poland will also accompany them to Bucharest. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

German Troops Reinforce Western Front to Stop French Advance, Only Localized Contact on the Front Line 17

Paris According to French sources, the results of the French artillery's first bombardment of the Siegfried Line are very satisfactory based on aerial photographs taken before and after the bombardment. However, it confirms the theory that many forts on the Siegfried Line were hastily built with inferior cement. According to a semi-official report reviewing the situation on the Western Front two weeks after the war, the French army advanced 20 kilometers along the entire front between the Rhine and Moselle rivers, in front of the Maginot Line, extending into Germany, and ensuring the absolute integrity of French territory. The German army is holding firmly to its positions on the Siegfried Line, and its progressively defensive outposts are now gradually benefiting from the situation on the Eastern Front. Germany is now sending elite troops and some air force from east to west to stop the French advance. According to the latest communique issued by the French High Command, there are no important developments worth mentioning on the front line, and air force activity has been reduced due to weather conditions. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

London A statement issued by the Information Department yesterday stated, "The great battle on the Western Front has yet to begin." The French High Command is fighting according to a detailed plan and is still in the reconnaissance period. (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Paris The High Command recently issued its 28th war bulletin, stating, "There were no important developments on the front line yesterday. Both sides' air forces had little activity due to bad weather." (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Berlin A communique from the German High Command stated that the French army's attack on the Zweibrücken area on the Western Front has been repelled by the German army with heavy losses. It is reported that the German army has occupied Dehlingen. (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Paris The High Command recently issued its 29th war bulletin, stating, "The entire line was calm last night, with only localized contact." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Paris According to reliable sources, the French army on the Western Front recently captured two German civilians for the first time. It is said that they were unaware that war had broken out between Germany and France. In addition, the French army also captured several German soldiers who had leaflets distributed by British aircraft to the German people in their pockets. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Berlin Foreign newspapers reported that the garrison of Aachen (also known as Aix-la-Chapelle) on the German border had been withdrawn. However, a report received here this afternoon stated that not only had the German troops not withdrawn, but there was no intention to withdraw. Several hospitals in the area had patients moved to other places last week so that the hospitals could be used for military purposes. The rumor that the German army was withdrawing from the area probably arose from this. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

German War Reports 18

Berlin – The German News Agency just released a general headquarters war report, stating roughly that "the war situation on the Polish front is nearing its end. The city of Lviv in the southeastern part of the country has been completely surrounded by our forces. The city of Lublin has also been captured. The line held by our forces on the eastern front starts from Lviv, passes through Volodymyr-Volynskyi, Brest-Litovsk, and goes north to Białystok. As for our forces in southern Poland, they are advancing towards Sokal, Rava-Ruska, and Krasnystaw. Therefore, the retreat route of the Polish army east of Lublin has been cut off. Furthermore, there is currently no trace of the Polish air force on any front line. Our air force has completed its mission on the eastern front. Multiple squadrons and a portion of artillery units have been ordered to concentrate in preparation for other tasks. Apart from this, there are no significant battles on the western front. Near Saarbrücken, our forces shot down a French aircraft. There were no air raids over our country." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Berlin – The German High Command issued a statement this afternoon stating that military operations within Poland are nearing completion. After surrounding Lviv and occupying Lublin, the German army's front line extends from Lviv to Volodymyr-Volynskyi, to Brest-Litovsk, to Białystok. In other words, the German-occupied area has exceeded half of Polish territory. The Polish army has been defeated by the German forces, scattered in many places, and lost contact. One of the strongest armies, accounting for about a quarter of the total force, is now trapped in the southwest corner of Wistne-rode, between the Vistula and Bzura rivers. Since yesterday, this army has shown signs of collapse. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

Polish Forces Continue to Resist Courageously. Foreign Minister Beck Delivers a Speech. 19

Paris – According to French news from Lublin, although the German army is superior in numbers and equipment, the Polish army is still fighting valiantly on all fronts. Their morale and the spirit of the Polish government and people remain consistent and unwavering. It is reported that President Mościcki has sent a telegram, entrusted to the ambassador in Rome to convey to President Roosevelt, stating that in the past few days, German aircraft have deliberately and systematically bombed towns with clearly no military objectives, resulting in thousands of civilian casualties. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Bucharest, Romania – The Polish Consulate in Cernăuți, Romania, issued a statement stating that Polish forces are currently engaged in fierce battles with both German and Soviet forces on all fronts. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Cernăuți, Romania – Foreigners arriving here from Poland report that Polish forces are resisting the German army along the line of Białystok, Brest, Lublin, Warsaw, Lviv, and Stryi in the east. The northern front is commanded by General Sosnkowski, the southern front by General Sikorski, and the central front in Warsaw by General Rommel. Polish air force pilots are extremely brave, often fighting against ten opponents without retreating. Furthermore, Soviet Ambassador to Poland, Sharikov, had a lengthy conversation with Foreign Minister Beck several days ago and then hastily returned to Moscow. At that time, it was still heard that he was planning to return to his post, but it has been five or six days without any news. Soviet troops have also entered Poland. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

London – Polish Foreign Minister Colonel Beck delivered a broadcast speech to the world last night from "somewhere in the southeastern part of the country," stating roughly that "the German army has seventy divisions, which are quite strong, and their air force and mechanized units also have an advantage. However, fierce battles are continuing on all sections of the front line. Although the Germans are using barbaric methods to bomb undefended cities, villages, and railway lines, the Polish army's ability to resist has not diminished in the slightest. Therefore, final victory will undoubtedly belong to the Allied forces. In short, the spirit of the Polish government, its army, and its people has not changed in the slightest and will certainly be maintained." (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Traffic Resumes Between Berlin and Danzig 20

Berlin – The express train between Berlin and Danzig is scheduled to resume today. The railway between Danzig and Lauenburg is currently only being used by the military authorities. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

Danzig – Germany recently began constructing a highway within the area of the former Free City of Danzig today to connect with the transportation lines of East Prussia. (Haitong News Agency dispatch on the 18th)

Daladier Inspects Front Line Situation 21

Paris – Premier and Minister of National Defense Daladier went to the eastern front yesterday to inspect the war situation and toured the positions in the German Saar region occupied by French troops. He has now returned to the city and is extremely satisfied with the war situation and the brave fighting and discipline of the frontline soldiers. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Warsaw: Negotiations Between Attacking and Defending Forces Regarding Civilian Evacuation. German Side Presents Several Conditions. Representatives from Both Armies Have Not Yet Met. 22

Zurich, Switzerland – German radio broadcast a message at 6:00 PM, stating roughly that the commander of the Warsaw defenses has sent a representative to contact the German commander to discuss the evacuation of civilians, foreign nationals, and diplomatic personnel from Warsaw. The German commander immediately received him and presented the following conditions: (1) Civilians, foreign nationals, and diplomatic personnel should each elect a representative, who will travel in three cars at 10:00 PM via the Praga town and Minsk highway to the German outpost. (2) All cars should have their lights on and display a white flag. (3) The Polish authorities should order their troops to cease fire on both sides of the highway for a distance of two kilometers. The German army also agrees to do the same. After the Warsaw defense commander accepts the above conditions, they should be confirmed via radio broadcast. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Berlin – According to a report last night, the German threat to Warsaw has been slightly delayed because the commander of the Polish garrison in Warsaw sent an envoy to meet with the German commander. The report did not mention whether the Polish commander had accepted the German ultimatum to surrender within twelve hours. The German army threatened the people of Warsaw that if they did not surrender, they would destroy the entire city with artillery and bombs. (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Cernowitz – Refugees who escaped from Warsaw by plane and arrived here today stated, "The situation in Warsaw is extremely chaotic. Military figures have strongly advised the city's defense commander to request a meeting with the German commander's special envoy." After sending a telegram, the German army immediately replied, expressing acceptance. The city's residents were filled with new hope. However, the reason why the special envoys of the Polish and German armies have not yet been able to meet is said to be that there is no responsible authority for military and political affairs in Warsaw, making it impossible to send representatives. In addition, Warsaw's food supplies are about to run out. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

Berlin – On the 17th, Polish radio broadcast a request for the German commander to meet with Warsaw officials carrying a truce flag. The German commander indicated his willingness to meet, but they had not arrived by late at night. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

Zhang Qun's Observation: Soviet-Japanese Non-Aggression Pact Unlikely 23

Chongqing – Zhang Qun, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Secretary-General of the Supreme National Defense Council, told an Associated Press reporter that Soviet-Japanese compromise faces numerous obstacles, making a non-aggression treaty unlikely. "It is a mistake to judge Soviet-Japanese relations based on Soviet-German relations. The Soviet Union and Germany have no deep-seated animosity, and their historical relationship has always been friendly. As for the Soviet Union and Japan, they have always been in a hostile and antagonistic position." This is the biggest difference. Zhang Qun also said that the Soviet Union did propose a non-aggression treaty to Japan three years ago, but Japan rejected it at the time because Japan has always regarded the Soviet Union as a thorn in its side, and Japan has been the most active in anti-communist activities. Furthermore, even if a non-aggression treaty is concluded, Japan will definitely withdraw its troops, while the Soviet Union will still retain its defensive forces stationed in the Far East. This is another reason why it is difficult to reach an agreement. As for the war against China, it has not intensified so far, but the Japanese plans are difficult to predict. As of now, the Japanese military actions in China are nothing more than strengthening their garrison position in Central China. It is expected that they will not take any major offensive actions in the short term. Not only that, the Japanese are now deeply aware that the front line is too long and vulnerable to our attacks, so they have taken steps to shorten their front line. In Guangdong, the Japanese front line has already been shortened, but they still cannot "eliminate" the Chinese guerrillas entering and exiting the Japanese front line. The Japanese action of shortening the front line proves that the Japanese forces are currently insufficient to maintain their long lines of communication. They are feeling insufficient to maintain the strength of the rear lines of communication. How can they have the strength to make a final offensive to resolve the war? However, the current Japanese are clearly trying to divide China's political groups and exploit China's resources to conquer China. Zhang Qun finally said that the European war not only has no impact on Sino-American relations, but also strengthens the relationship between the two countries. The difficulty is that the United States talks more than it acts. In fact, the United States has enough strength to dominate the balance of power in the Far East. (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Soviet and Japanese Military Representatives Meet Again 24

Nomonhan – Representatives of the Japanese and Soviet armies at Nomonhan held a second preliminary negotiation at 5:00 PM on the 17th on the grasslands between the two armies' positions on the banks of the Khalkha River. The Japanese representatives were Lieutenant Colonel Tanaka, Major Irimura, and interpreter Ando. The Soviet side had Major General Potapov and one colonel, two majors, two captains, one second lieutenant, and one Mongolian major, a total of eight people. Major General Potapov first responded to the Japanese proposal from yesterday, saying that they had been ordered by the central government to be appointed as local ceasefire negotiating commissioners, and they hoped to start ceasefire negotiations as soon as possible. As a result of the agreement between the two representatives, it was decided to hold the first official negotiation at 4:00 PM on the 18th at the same venue as the meeting on the 17th. The second preliminary negotiation was completed in a peaceful atmosphere at 6:10 PM. (Domei dispatch on the 17th)

Hailar – The official negotiations between the two armies on the spot over the disputes on the Manchukuo border started at 4:00 PM on the 18th. After the meeting, according to the Tōgō ambassador and Molotov agreement, each side will appoint two members to organize the Manchukuo border demarcation committee. Before the establishment of the committee, various negotiations will continue in Moscow. After the committee is completed, the contact point for both parties to negotiate local affairs seems to be designated as the Manchuria place. (Domei dispatch on the 18th)

Tokyo – The Foreign Ministry spokesman said this morning while hosting reporters, that he had the impression that the principle of resolving the Nomonhan incident could be extended to other parts of the border. When reporters asked whether a non-aggression pact could be concluded due to the border agreement, the spokesman replied that he did not have such a treaty in mind at the moment. The existing ceasefire agreement has nothing to do with the European situation. Japan does not want to interfere in the European war, but wants to concentrate its energy on resolving the China Incident. Therefore, Japan is prepared to enter into agreements with any other country regarding various outstanding issues, but it does not intend to conclude a non-aggression pact with the Soviet Union at present. There are many unresolved issues between the Soviet Union and Japan. If they are resolved one by one, it may not be necessary to conclude a non-aggression pact. However, no one can say what will happen in the future. When a reporter asked who first proposed the ceasefire agreement, the spokesman said that this issue arose when Ambassador Tōgō to the Soviet Union and Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov discussed various outstanding issues. The spokesman did not want to say anything about the future, but said that everything depends on the results of the work of the demarcation committee. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Tokyo – According to a Foreign Ministry spokesman, the rumor that the German government is involved in the Nomonhan ceasefire agreement is not true. This agreement is purely a local incident. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Terauchi and His Entourage Arrive in Berlin 25

Berlin – Former Japanese Army Minister General Terauchi, accompanied by three senior staff officers, arrived here from Italy tonight. Those who welcomed him at the station included Assistant Harlem from the Protocol Department, Counselor Knorr, a Far East expert from the Foreign Ministry, and Lieutenant General Seifert, Commander of the Berlin Military Region. (Haitong dispatch on the 17th)

Japanese Industry Suffers a Blow 26

Washington – According to a US Department of Commerce official today, Japan's industrial expansion plan in the "Yen Bloc" region, including its "Manchuria" development plan, will be severely hit by the outbreak of the European war, which has cut off the supply of machinery and equipment from Germany and Italy. At the same time, rising foreign raw material prices will also hinder the implementation of this plan. (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

Italian Foreign Minister Receives Polish Ambassador 27

Rome – Italian Foreign Minister Ciano met with Polish Ambassador to Italy Długoszowski last night. According to well-informed sources, the discussion revolved around the Soviet Union's invasion of Poland. (Haitong dispatch on the 18th)

US Government Closely Watches Changes in the European Situation. Roosevelt Cancels Vacation. Newspapers Criticize Brutal Aggression. 28

Washington – US President Roosevelt originally planned to take a yacht to the Potomac yesterday to spend the usual weekend vacation, but he temporarily cancelled it due to the sudden invasion of Poland by Soviet troops. He spent the whole day discussing European issues with senior State Department officials. Secretary of State Hull also studied the reports of diplomatic representatives in his office and informed the President of the situation at any time. The special session of Congress is scheduled to be held this Thursday, and the President will exchange views with congressional leaders on the eve of the meeting. Currently, US officials are unwilling to express any opinion on the Soviet Union's actions. According to isolationist Senator Borah, "European borders have nothing to do with us." (Associated Press dispatch on the 18th)

New York – The local newspapers unanimously condemned the Soviet troops' entry into Poland, saying that Hitler and Stalin used the same brutal methods of aggression. The New York Post stated, "At this moment, no one in the United States should simply shrug their shoulders and say that the United States 'must isolate itself from the European war, and everything else is not worth considering.' Those isolationists claim that American interests will not be threatened under any circumstances. We dare not agree with this statement. The world is brewing major changes, and we must earnestly pray that these changes will not threaten our country, thereby forcing us to deal with it with force. It is true, but to say that these changes will not pose any threat to our country is also blind protection. If we obstruct it in many ways, so that our country cannot use its influence to cope with future events, it will be foolishness." The New York Times stated, "Stalin has betrayed Britain and France and concluded a non-aggression pact with Germany. The price he has obtained is the invasion of Poland by his troops. The Soviet government is no different from acting as a running dog for the German lion. However, even if Germany and the Soviet Union form an alliance, it may not be detrimental to the democratic countries, because once those countries get too close, their mutual suspicion will arise spontaneously. Hitlerism has been mixed with communism, and Stalinism has been mixed with fascism. The whole world also knows that the so-called ideological problem is nothing more than a struggle between democratic freedom, peace and authoritarian terror." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

British and French Public Opinion 29

London – Renowned journalist Price recently published an article in the Daily Mail, commenting on the Soviet troops' entry into Poland. The gist of his words is that this kind of "unholy" alliance is too unnatural and unlikely to be effective. It may even bring disaster to Germany and the Soviet Union. He said, "The cooperation between the Soviet Union and Germany is definitely not limited to safeguarding the interests of each country. It can be asserted that Germany will never want the Soviet Union's land and air forces to cooperate with it on the front line in Poland. It is unimaginable for national socialist troops and Bolshevik troops to fight side by side in any part of the world. Moreover, there are not a few communists in Germany. If the Soviet Union takes the opportunity to carry out red propaganda in Germany, the crisis will be too great for Germany to tolerate. Based on this, the combination of Germany and the Soviet Union is too unnatural and unlikely to be effective. It may even bring disaster to each country." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Paris – The local newspapers commented on the Soviet troops' entry into Poland, unanimously expressing extreme indignation. The comments in Le Petit Parisien best represent the general view. It is said that "force and shamelessness have gained the upper hand. How can we allow this situation to continue? Judging from the past, this kind of action will eventually be rewarded. Britain and France will only do their best to uphold justice." L'Aube stated, "The reasons put forward by Stalin are not worth considering. The non-aggression pact previously concluded between Germany and the Soviet Union is in the name of non-aggression, but in reality it is about invading Poland. This is cruel and ridiculous. However, it is not impossible for the Soviet Union to take surprising actions against Germany in the future, even greater than what the country has inflicted on Britain and France during negotiations in Moscow. It is disappointing and dangerous for the Soviet Union to pursue this kind of diplomacy and use this kind of strategy, but Britain and France's determination to prevent Hitler and his partners from harming the whole world will not be shaken. Poland should still have confidence in its allies and friends and should have unwavering faith in its glorious future." Renowned journalist Pertinax published an article in L'Ordre, stating roughly that "as far as we can see, the Soviet Union's current policy aims to expand its territory, just as Imperial Russia did. In essence, the country wants to recover the provinces it previously lost. However, it is difficult to say whether it will take the opportunity to seize Bessarabia from Romania as revenge. However, after Germany and the Soviet Union divide the spoils, how their relationship will evolve is a matter of great interest." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

National Political Council: Fourth Session Discusses Various Proposals, Passes 77 Recommendations and 5 Provisional Motions, with the Most Important Being the Sichuan-Kangding Development Plan and the Constitutional Proposal 30

Chongqing – The Fourth Session of the National Political Council in Chongqing, which opened on the 9th, lasted for ten days. Several plenary meetings were held, resulting in extremely satisfactory outcomes and abundant gains. In addition to those who attended the opening ceremony on the 9th, the following members of the Council successively arrived to attend this session: Hu Yuan-yan, Zhang Zhongfu,晏陽初, Tan Pingshan, Li Xiangen, Cheng Shewo, Chang Naihui, Liu Wang Liming, Yu Yuzhi, Zhong Rongguang, Zhang Shizhao, Liang Shangdong, Mo Dehui, Wang Zhixin, Wu Yifang, Li Yuanding, Tao Baichuan, and others, totaling 141 people, which is more than the number of participants in the previous two sessions, fully demonstrating the spirit of national unity and concerted effort to overcome national difficulties. At the first, second, third, and fourth meetings, the Council listened to the report of the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Inspection Group and the reports of the heads of the Executive Yuan and various ministries and commissions on the political, military, economic, financial, transportation, diplomatic, internal affairs, and educational situations over the past six months. The Council conducted detailed discussions and concrete suggestions on these reports. The fifth, sixth, seventh, eighth, and ninth meetings were devoted to discussing various proposals. A total of 84 recommendations were made by the Council members at this session, of which 77 were passed by the Council. In addition, five provisional motions were also passed. The Council also elected Kong Geng, Zhang Lan, Li Zhongxiang, Gao Xibing, Zhang Junmai, Xu Xiaoyan, Zuo Shunsheng, Chen Shao, Chen Bosheng, Chu Fucheng, Hang Liwu, Xirao Gyatso, Lin Hu, Fan Yusui, Hu Shiqing, Deng Feihuang, Liu Shumo, Leng Tou, Huang Yanpei, Xu Deheng, Lu Qian, Li Huang, Shi Liang, Dong Biwu, Jiang Yong, Qin Bangxian, and 25 others as resident members during the Fourth Session. Liu Shimin, the originally elected member, resigned from the position to the Speaker on the spot, and Qin Bangxian was elected by a majority vote to fill the vacancy. Among the resolutions of this session, the most important were the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Plan and the request to the government to issue an explicit order to convene the National Assembly on a fixed date to formulate a constitution and implement constitutional government. In addition, the actions of traitors, which were deeply hated and abhorred by the Chinese people, were also resolved by the Council, and a nationwide telegram was sent in the name of the Council to denounce them. In addition, two provisional motions were also passed: (1) to express condolences to the soldiers at the front and the compatriots in the war zone in the name of the Council; (2) to issue a letter of condolences to the Northeast compatriots in the name of the Council. (18th dispatch)

Proposal to Convene the National Assembly

Chongqing – Regarding the proposal to request the government to convene the National Assembly on a fixed date to formulate a constitution and implement constitutional government, it was the result of seven proposals submitted by 52 Council members including Kong Geng, 26 Council members including Chen Shaoyu, 36 Council members including Zuo Shunsheng, 40 Council members including Jiang Hengyuan, 21 Council members including Zhang Shenfu, 37 Council members including Wang Zaoshi, and 55 Council members including Zhang Junli, which were merged for review and thoroughly discussed. It was resolved that two methods, fundamental and stopgap, were unanimously passed by the Council. The case is recorded as follows:

(A) Fundamental Measures: (1) Request the government to issue an explicit order to convene the National Assembly on a fixed date to formulate a constitution and implement constitutional government; (2) The Speaker shall designate a number of Council members to form a Constitutional Government Promotion Committee of the National Political Council to assist the government in promoting constitutional government.

(B) Stopgap Measures: (1) Request the government to issue a clear declaration that all Chinese people, except traitors, are equal in political status under the law; (2) In order to meet the needs of wartime, the government's administrative organs should be strengthened and reformed to concentrate talents from all over the country to engage in the work of resisting the war and building the nation, and to seek final victory. (18th dispatch)

Content of the Sichuan-Kangding Development Plan

Chongqing – The Sichuan-Kangding Development Plan was formulated by the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Promotion Committee based on the report of the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Inspection Group. This plan has been submitted by the Speaker to the Council for discussion and has been unanimously passed, and it has been sent to the government for earnest implementation. The general explanation and attached recommendations are recorded as follows: (General Explanation of the Sichuan-Kangding Development Plan) The Sichuan-Kangding Construction Promotion Committee was established after the Speaker's proposal was passed by the Third Session. Subsequently, the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Inspection Group was organized, with 21 Council members designated by the Speaker to form five groups for the East Road, South Road, West Road, North Road, and Xikang, respectively. They departed successively in March and returned to Chongqing in July. Each group submitted an inspection report, and after several meetings, the results of the discussions on various topics were compiled into this plan. It should be stated that the sole basis of this plan is the report of the Sichuan-Kangding Construction Inspection Group. This report is the result of the efforts of more than 20 Council members over more than 100 days. All the problems raised were discovered through on-the-spot inspections, and all the methods advocated were based on the requirements of the facts. The Sichuan and Kangding provinces have vast territories, complex ethnic groups, and local conditions that vary from place to place. What one has may be what the other lacks (for example, drug prohibition). One may be considered excessive, while the other may be considered insufficient (for example, the powers of officials below the county magistrate). The inspection group respected the facts, and the promotion committee followed suit. What exists should not be omitted, and what does not exist should not be fabricated. Therefore, after opening the book, one may inevitably feel that it is messy, which is different from general plans that are based on theory and are brilliantly prepared. This should be stated first. The source of the information in this plan has some value that is cherished by people. Those who read this plan should pursue its origin one by one, otherwise, they will not understand its intention, or even suspect that it is moaning without being sick. Therefore, it is necessary to first check the overview of opinions listed in Chapter 3 of Section 1 of the report, and then check the original text of the report according to its annotations. Then the source is clear, and there is no fear of being superficial when judging. This should be stated second. This plan is rich in content and the clues are inevitably more complicated. If it is resolved and passed and implemented by the government one by one, it would be a great blessing. However, what we hope for is in the major points. Those that are sufficient to establish the foundation of construction, or sufficient to constitute obstacles to construction, we hope that the government will make wise decisions and resolutely promote or reform them. Then all difficulties will surely be solved easily. Furthermore, considering that laws cannot be implemented by themselves, and that there are people who govern before there are laws to govern, the issue of the selection of personnel who implement all policies deserves special attention. The Council members deeply know that the government has a painful intention in employing people, but at the same time, they deeply believe that the government's employment of people will never leave obstacles to the progress of reform for the sake of temporary and tactful compromises. The Council members are more willing to add two points: (1) This case focuses on the construction of Sichuan and Kangding, but the methods advocated in the case and the facts on which they are based are not unique to Sichuan and Kangding. If the government believes that it is necessary for general provinces to adopt them, it is hoped that the implementation will not be limited to Sichuan and Kangding; (2) Browsing through the inspection report, it is all-encompassing. All the records are rare anecdotes that are difficult to obtain at ordinary times. Often, the facts of a certain time and place contain the blood and tears of countless people, and the life of the nation and the nation is attacked. However, it is not entirely recorded in the proposal. It is hoped that the authorities of various ministries and commissions will take the inspection report and read it as a strong reference material. The colleagues feel the heavy responsibility of the rear area in the War of Resistance, the urgent call of the people, and the urgent need for local construction. They sincerely hope for this. The content of this proposal is divided into (1) Administrative Organization, (2) Military Service, (3) Finance and People's Livelihood, (4) Public Security, (5) Economic Construction, (6) Drug Prohibition, (7) Education, (8) Yi Affairs, (9) Judicial Part of the Sichuan-Kangding Border Area. (18th dispatch)

Shiqi Was Bombed by Japanese Planes Yesterday 36

Japanese Auto Repair Shop in Bian Completely Burned Down 37

Xi'an – On the night of the 9th, a Chinese army team sneaked into Kaifeng City and burned down the Japanese auto repair shop in front of the Japanese Lishi Tingmen. At that time, the fire broke out everywhere and burned all night. The Japanese were extremely panicked, and the fire was extinguished until the morning of the 10th. The factory and houses were completely burned down, several people were killed or injured, six cars were destroyed, and more than 100 boxes of gasoline were destroyed. Two Japanese firms were also destroyed. The team then sneaked into the repair shop at Zhihai Station on the night of the 10th and completely blew up the repair machine room of the factory while the Japanese were unprepared. The explosion was like thunder, and the entire city was terrified. (17th dispatch)

Japanese Troops Landing on the South Bank of the Yangtze River in Northern Hunan Were Repelled, Japanese Losses Were Extremely Heavy, Chinese Had Slight Casualties 38

Changde – More than 100 Japanese soldiers landed on the Xinhekou river bank, more than 50 miles west of Chenglingji, at 6 a.m. on the 17th, and engaged in fierce fighting with our defending troops. Another group of more than 200 people, riding in four Japanese boats, sneaked to the vicinity of Sanzhaojiao, about three miles west of Xinhekou, at noon, and also forcibly landed under the cover of artillery fire, making contact with the Chinese army. At the same time, four Japanese warships and four speedboats, carrying more than 100 Japanese soldiers, attempted to sail up the Yangtze River. At noon, they arrived at Zhongjiamen near Huang Gongmiao (three miles west of Sanzhaojiao). The Japanese warships on the river bank stopped there, and the four speedboats continued to move west, cruising around Guangxingzhou, northwest of Huang Gongmiao, for a while, and then turned back, staying in the river in Zhongjiamen. The Japanese warships fired more than ten shells at the Japanese army on the opposite bank, destroying several civilian houses. Before long, the Japanese soldiers on the ship landed there and also clashed with the Chinese army. After the Japanese soldiers landed in Xinhekou, Sanzhaojiao, and Zhongjiamen on the south bank of the Yangtze River, they launched a fierce battle along the river with the Chinese defense forces. The Japanese troops in Xinhekou and Sanzhaojiao were fiercely attacked by the Chinese army and were defeated and retreated by 9 p.m. The Japanese warships fled to the east. The Japanese troops in Zhongjiamen fought fiercely through the night. By 8 a.m. on the 18th, they could not stand on the shore due to repeated pressure from the Chinese army, and fled back to the warships one after another. The Japanese troops who had landed in various places have been completely repelled by the Chinese army. Only two Japanese warships and four speedboats are still cruising in the river near Zhongjiamen. The Chinese garrison is still closely monitoring the situation. In this battle, the Japanese army suffered a severe blow from the Chinese army, with heavy casualties. Zhao Zhenping, the battalion commander of a certain Chinese battalion, and Zhu Moshang, the company commander, were injured by stray bullets because they personally commanded the battle on the front line. Soldiers also suffered slight casualties. (18th dispatch)

U.S. Protests Against Japanese Bombing Case 39

Peiping – The U.S. Embassy yesterday formally protested to the Japanese Embassy regarding the Japanese army's bombing of American commercial interests in China six times in August. The most recent bombing took place in Yangjiang, Guangdong, where property of the American Catholic Church was hit by four bombs dropped by Japanese planes on August 18, all within 100 yards, causing minor damage. (18th Associated Press dispatch)

Soviet Ambassador Visits U.S. Ambassador 40

Chongqing – The newly appointed Soviet Ambassador to China, Pan Youxin, has now formally visited the diplomatic representatives of other countries in China. Yesterday, he visited U.S. Ambassador Johnson, and Johnson also returned the visit. It is now learned that Pan came to China as part of the Soviet trade mission, but not long after arriving in China, he was appointed by Moscow as the ambassador to China. (18th Reuters dispatch)

Hong Kong Controls Foreign Exchange Supplementary Regulations 41

Hong Kong – The Hong Kong government today announced two supplementary regulations for foreign exchange control: (1) Foreign currency may be purchased from foreign exchange exchanges designated by the Hong Kong government for legitimate commercial purposes; (2) All Chinese banks registered with the Hong Kong government may sell Chinese national currency and may manage remittances between Hong Kong and the mainland, subject to restrictions and in accordance with the rules promulgated by the Hong Kong government. (17th dispatch)

Finance: Gold Prices Plunge After Rising Amid Rumors, Reaching a High of 380 Yuan in the Morning, Selling Frenzy Leads to Closing Price of 4,000 Yuan 42

Yesterday, the cash gold dark market situation suddenly became huge again. It was exceptionally strong in the early morning, but tended to fall sharply in the afternoon. As a result, it plunged by 190 yuan. Initially, it was believed that the signing of the truce agreement between Japan and the Soviet Union and Mongolia was unfavorable to China, so it opened sharply at 4,300 yuan in the morning. Subsequently, rumors arose frequently, and foreign exchange gradually strengthened, so a selling frenzy was triggered. Pawnshops continued to sell, and some securities firms and gold shops also followed suit. The trend immediately turned downward and soon fell back to 4,105 yuan. No Development on the Defense Area Issue, Situation in Western Shanghai Still Serious, Many Rumours in the City, Difficult to Verify, Concession Authorities Consider and Respond Cautiously 56

Regarding the negotiations on the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries and the Japanese side's request to adjust the defense area, many rumors have been circulating for days, but it is difficult to verify. This morning, it was widely rumored in the city that the British defense area north of the Suzhou River had been transferred to the Japanese side. This newspaper inquired from various parties, but it was difficult to obtain definite news. The British Embassy also denied the matter. In order to investigate the truth, this reporter personally went to the north bank of the Suzhou River to observe at 2:00 AM this morning. The sentry posts on the Tianhou Palace Bridge and the Garbage Bridge were still on duty as usual. The Tian Tong Road and Suzhou River Road area was quiet because it was late at night and in a state of curfew, so no police or patrol officers were seen. At that time, the area was quiet and there was no unusual phenomenon. In addition, it was rumored that the police power of the Great Western Road had also been transferred to the puppet "City Government". However, according to this newspaper's investigation, it is known that yesterday was the 9/18 Anniversary, and in order to avoid conflicts, the police reduced the number of patrols and there was no other intention. However, the concession authorities are responding cautiously to the current situation. The news obtained yesterday is described in detail as follows:

No Proposals Yet for Adjusting Defense Area

According to well-informed foreign sources, on the 13th of this month, Japanese Marine Corps Commander ______ Hu convened a meeting of the commanders of the British, American, and Italian forces stationed in Shanghai. The purpose was to seek the consent of the commanders of various countries to adjust the defense areas of the forces stationed in Shanghai. However, during the meeting, the Japanese side did not propose a specific adjustment plan, and none of the commanders present had any intention of proposing a specific plan. So Commander ______ Hu of Japan stated that if the countries agreed, the Japanese side would propose a specific proposal as the basis for future discussions. However, as of now, the Japanese side has not yet submitted a plan, and it has not been able to reach a compromise with the British side. The United States is willing to be the backing of the United Kingdom, and has repeatedly stated that it does not want to change the status of Shanghai. The firm attitude of the responsible officials stationed in Shanghai has made Japan wary and unable to rashly add military pressure. However, under the current circumstances, it is very possible for Japan to intensify its use of political tactics in an attempt to obtain greater rights and interests from the concession, such as the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries. Although it is not true that the patrols of the Shanghai Municipal Council in the area of road construction beyond the boundaries in western Shanghai have automatically withdrawn, as claimed by the Japanese newspapers, the issue of road construction beyond the boundaries will eventually be resolved in ten days or half a month. As for the rumors that Japan will block the British defense area from the North Jiangxi Road to the North Xizang Road, it is feared that it is due to a misunderstanding. The Japanese side wants to take over the British defense area of ​​Section A (North Section) of North Jiangxi Road, but the British side has not agreed, so there is such a rumour.

Checking Commuters and Vehicles

Obstacles were placed on Haige Road in the area of road construction beyond the boundaries, such as the Yuyuan Road intersection, the Jing'an Temple Road intersection, the Great Western Road intersection, and the Foch Road intersection, leaving only a narrow entrance for entry and exit. More than ten Chinese and Western detectives and members of the International Volunteer Corps were stationed at each location, checking commuters and vehicles very strictly. From Difeng Road to Xujiahui, such as the Foch Road, Itingpan Road, and Xiafei Road intersections, Chinese and Western detectives were also stationed, and an armored vehicle and a patrol car were patrolling the aforementioned areas. However, the side door of the Lin family mansion at 448 Haige Road was closed yesterday, and only the main door was used for entry and exit. Six puppet policemen were stationed at the door, and the situation was more serious than before.

Volunteer Corps Patrolling Roads Beyond Boundaries

From Haige Road to Anhe Temple Road on the Great Western Road, Volunteer Corps members were constantly patrolling in military trucks. Three puppet police officers were stationed at both ends of the Fahua Bridge, checking pedestrians very strictly. In front of the puppet police substation at the Columbia Road intersection, there were originally two puppet police officers guarding, but yesterday it had been increased to six. At the staff dormitory of Shanghai Commercial Bank at 1760 Jing'an Temple Road, six puppet police officers were still stationed, and the situation was the same as before, with no major changes. At the entrance of the Shining New Village in the Siming Villa on Pingyuan Road, there were originally two puppet police officers guarding, but yesterday it was reduced to one. However, at the Qianjia Alley intersection opposite Yuguang Village, the number of puppet police officers stationed had increased to eight, and the situation had become tighter.

Puppet Police Penetrate Into Brenan Road

The two places between 1249 and the opposite Ivans-Tai Dance Hall are the staff dormitories of the Japanese-owned Toyota Yarn Factory. There were no puppet police officers stationed there before, but yesterday two people were also sent to guard them. At the Brenan Road intersection of Zhaofeng Park, six puppet police officers were suddenly found to be stationed yesterday morning, and all commuters were surprised to see it. Recently, the police have dispatched fewer police officers to patrol, but yesterday they specially increased patrols, and armored troops also patrolled from time to time.

Triangular Area Completely Blocked

The situation in the triangular area at the intersection of Jassfield Road and Avenue Haig on yesterday was even more tense. All entrances and exits were almost completely blocked by barbed wire. A large number of Italian soldiers and Chinese and Western detectives were stationed there, leaving only a small gap for commuters to pass through, while vehicles of all kinds were not allowed to pass. Therefore, the No. 7 bus had to be diverted. The inspections of commuters were extremely strict, and the situation was very serious. Barbed wire was set up at the Jiaozhou Road Xinzha Road intersection, the Robert Sheng Road intersection, and the Kangnaut Road Yanping Road intersection. More than ten Italian soldiers and Chinese and Western detectives were stationed there, and the guard was also very strict. The defense in the Caojiadu area was quite lax yesterday, and even the puppet police were not seen much. There were only a few sentry police officers. However, the buses on the upper roads and the trolley buses on the 16th and 19th could not drive straight to Wujiaochang, and the situation was even more deserted.

Restriction of Businesses in the War Zone or Approaching War Zone

In order to maintain the original organization of profit-making legal entities in the war zone, the Ministry of Economic Affairs has formulated temporary measures for maintaining the status quo of profit-making legal entities during extraordinary times and announced them for implementation. The measures stipulate that profit-making legal entities in the war zone or approaching the war zone shall maintain their original status. The convening of shareholders' meetings and the re-election of directors and supervisors shall be postponed. The original directors and supervisors shall not be relieved of their responsibilities during the postponement. The purpose is to prevent traitors from interfering and causing the businesses to be destroyed. Since its implementation, it has had considerable success. However, it only maintains the inherent organization of profit-making individuals, and has not uniformly restricted the transfer, mortgage, or change of the rights and interests of various businesses. The scope of use of its assets and restrictions on entering into joint ventures with foreign merchants have not yet been stipulated, and it is still insufficient to maintain and protect the energy to the fullest. After presentation to the Executive Yuan, approval was granted to stipulate five measures for restricting various businesses in the war zone or approaching the war zone.

1. The changing of the names of various fishery rights holders and mining rights holders or the transfer, mortgage, or change of their rights and interests, as well as the changing of the names of forestry contractors, state-owned mining rights lessees, or those who have obtained special business rights, shall all be submitted to the Ministry for approval. All those that have not been approved are invalid.

2. The premises and equipment of various farms, forest farms, pastures, fish farms, mining farms, factories, or companies, and the real estate invested in them, shall not be used for other purposes or mortgaged to others without being submitted to the Ministry for approval.

3. The transfer or mortgage of shares of various companies or the changing of shareholders' names shall all be reported to the Ministry for record. All those that have not been reported to the Ministry are invalid.

4. Various companies shall, in accordance with the law, fully deposit the public reserve fund in each term. All accumulated public reserve funds shall not be withdrawn or used without being submitted to the Ministry for approval, and shall be deposited in national banks. Those that have been deposited in registered commercial banks or local banks and are inconvenient to change the deposit shall also be submitted to the Ministry for approval and record.

5. All contracts or deeds entered into by various companies or other business organizers or representatives with foreign merchants regarding rights and interests shall be invalid unless approved by the Ministry. In addition to having sent a letter to the Ministry of Justice and Administration to forward to courts at all levels for notification, it has also been ordered to the construction halls of various provinces to implement the same.

9/18 Anniversary: Citizens Passed It Steadfastly, Public Concession More Heavily Guarded, Northwest Area Traffic Shortened, Alert Lifted Today 57

The public concession's defense deployment was cancelled within the national defense zone at 7 pm last night due to the good situation. However, armored cars continued to patrol, and the detective's inspection work along the way did not stop. Yesterday was the 8th anniversary of the fall of the three northeastern provinces. The police authorities of the Public Concession were deeply concerned about the occurrence of unexpected unfortunate events, so they took the necessary precautions a few days ago, including searching famous hotels, increasing patrol teams, and inspecting pedestrians. From the afternoon of the day before yesterday, they adopted the emergency measures that had been taken in the past, sealing off the intersections connected to the French Concession, setting up barriers, and cutting off traffic. Armored vehicles still set off from time to time to patrol, and the Public Concession Corps was only fully prepared. The order was peaceful throughout the day, and there were no disturbances until the evening. It is heard that the precautions will be lifted this morning, and all the blocked places on the roads will be opened. However, ordinary precautions will still be implemented as usual, and the western Shanghai area will also be closely guarded as before.

Methods for Transporting and Selling Silk: Clearance Based on Licenses and Certificates 60

Industry Association

to comply with, and have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and record. transportation of silk goods,

decided on the original plan, and telegraphed to various provincial governments instructing local competent authorities to allow customs distribution licenses and industry association certificates to be inspected and released. Printed Fractional Currency Notes to be Issued Soon; Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance Again to Expedite Release; Rumors of Reprinting New Currency are Untrue; Tram Fare Vouchers Should Not Be Used Elsewhere 61

Since the Shanghai branch of the Central Bank temporarily suspended the issuance of fractional currency notes, various companies and firms have indiscriminately issued their own printed fractional currency notes, and counterfeit cases have been discovered, leading to a gradual worsening of the problem. Small businesses are facing extreme difficulties, and the livelihood of the common people is greatly affected. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, deeply aware of this, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance again, stating, "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Chongqing, the fractional currency notes have not yet arrived, making it difficult to find change, greatly affecting the livelihood of the common people. Please immediately print and issue them as per the previous telegram. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce respectfully. " It is heard that the Shanghai branch of the Central Bank, due to sample drafts being leaked, temporarily suspended the issuance for the sake of caution. The head office has instructed the Hong Kong office to negotiate with Wing On Company nearby and thoroughly investigate the cause of the leak. It is heard that the negotiation is nearing completion, and the leaked sample drafts have been identified as few in number, so it has been decided to reissue the already printed fractional currency notes in the short term, but whether to add a stamp is still undetermined. Rumors of reprinting new currency are untrue.

Tram Fare

Vouchers are Lacking

Since the Shanghai branch of the Central Bank suspended the issuance of fractional currency notes, various shops in the city have successively issued fare vouchers to provide change. However, recently counterfeit vouchers have been rampant and are often refused. Merchants have switched to using the tram company's fare vouchers to maintain exchange, leading to a great demand for the tram company's fare vouchers, with a total issue amount reaching over 50,000 yuan.

Company Advises

Not to Use for Other Purposes

It is learned that the British-owned tram company in Shanghai has recently found that its fare vouchers are widely circulating in the market, causing ticket sellers to lack change and encounter many obstacles. Yesterday, it issued a notice to passengers, stating, "Tram fare vouchers can only be used on trams. Please advise residents not to use them elsewhere. This will greatly help our company's ticket sellers and provide more assistance to customers in finding change. Please cooperate to the best of your ability."

Flat-Price Rice Sales Continue as Usual Today; Over 1,800 Bags of Tribute Rice Sold in Two Days; Over 6,100 Bags Still Available for Flat-Price Sale 62

The five flat-price rice sales locations in the two concessions, with 8,000 bags of tribute rice, temporarily suspended flat-price sales yesterday due to a notification from the concession authorities that yesterday was the 9/18 Incident Memorial Day and a state of alert was in effect. However, civilians from all walks of life were not informed in advance. At 7:00 AM yesterday, they still carried baskets as usual to the nearest flat-price sales locations, waiting for the doors to open to purchase tickets and collect rice. It was decided that flat-price sales would continue as usual today. Upon receiving this news, the disappointed civilians returned home. as Usual Today

Rapid Development of Rich Resources in the Southwest; Strengthening the War of Resistance; The Rebirth of the Chinese Nation Has Already Taken Shape in the Interior 64

The Continental News reported that the vast southwestern provinces of China, with exceptionally rich and undeveloped resources, are attracting increasing attention from the world, according to the Credit Investigation Agency Bulletin. Since the Central Government moved its capital to Chongqing, the southwestern provinces, with a total area of 1,520,015 square kilometers and a population of 117 million, have been developed into a strong base for China's war of resistance. Recent reports reaching the outside world have clearly demonstrated the abundance of

natural resources

in this virgin land. Under the protection and encouragement of the government, rapid progress is underway, and the realized development, the scope of which is so large that it would hardly have been possible without the current war. It is expected that more news of the great development of this part of China will be heard in the future. China's industrial and financial resources, as well as various talents, have been concentrated in the southwestern provinces, and it is widely believed that the rebirth of the Chinese nation is now taking shape in this great interior. The southwestern provinces, including Xikang, have various

abundant minerals.

It is estimated that the region contains a total of 13,270,000 tons of coal reserves, including 12,104,000 tons of bituminous coal and the rest anthracite. Under the leadership of the government, mining operations have been actively undertaken. Among the southwestern provinces, Sichuan has the largest coal reserves, with a total of 9,874,000 tons of bituminous coal. Yunnan is second, with 1,485,000,000 tons of bituminous coal and 11 million tons of anthracite.

Guizhou is next

with a total coal production of 1,549,000 tons, including 77.5 million tons of bituminous coal and 77.4 million tons of anthracite. Guangxi's coal reserves reach 44 million tons of anthracite and 11.3 million tons of bituminous coal. The richest coal seam in Sichuan province originates from the Jialing River in the center of the province and follows the river south to Chongqing. Mineralogists estimate that the seam contains a total of 49.1 million tons of bituminous coal, which is well-suited for producing high-quality thermal coal. The upper reaches of the Minjiang River also have abundant coal reserves, reportedly reaching 17.6 million tons. The coal mines in the area can be easily

transported elsewhere

via the Minjiang River. The coal reserves in southern Sichuan are estimated at 33 million tons, but transportation is inconvenient in the area, making mining efforts difficult. It is reported that Yiliang in Yunnan province has a total coal reserve of 17 million tons. Since the city is located on the Yunnan-Vietnam Railway, transportation is very convenient, and the coal produced is sold throughout the province. When the Sichuan-Yunnan Railway is completed in 1940, the coal from Xuanwei in northern Yunnan will be able to compete with the coal produced in Yiliang. It is estimated that the Xuanwei area has 33 million tons of coal. In addition to coal,

the southwest is also rich in iron

The iron ore of the Yangtze River is known for its 12 million tons of high-quality iron sand. Not far from Dianjiang, there are also large iron deposits estimated at 33 million tons. Near Luding in eastern Xikang, there are 17 million tons of iron sand. Many other parts of this remote interior have also discovered rich ore deposits, which are now awaiting development. Benefiting from its convenient location and the natural resources in its vicinity, Chongqing has now become the center of China's economic and industrial life.

Freighters from Trieste to Shanghai and India

The Italian shipping company's postal ships, including the "Vittoriano Contarini," "Conte Biancamano," "Conte Rosso," and "Giulio Cesare," operated between Italy and Shanghai, and their business was very prosperous. Although the Eurasian routes of the warring countries such as Britain and France have not been completely cut off, merchants and passengers are apprehensive, so the Italian shipping company's passenger and freight transport has become twice as busy as before.

After Japanese Side Threatens Blockade, Shanghai-Wenzhou Route Suspended Again; New An Lee Ship Intercepted and Turned Back; Wing Tai Marler Ship Has Changed Route; Japanese Ships Transporting Japanese Goods and Drugs for Dumping in Likang 69

After the Shanghai-Wenzhou route was successfully tested by British ships, various ships successively set sail. However, the Japanese Navy suddenly announced the blockade of Wenzhou Bay starting on the evening of the 17th, causing the New An Lee ship to turn back after reaching Wenzhou. It is still difficult to predict whether the Shen You ship, which sailed out on the morning of the 17th, will reach its destination. After the German ships Mou Fu and Hanna on the Shanghai-Ningbo route returned to Shanghai, the Hanna ship was scheduled to sail to Ningbo as usual on the 22nd, but the opening date of the Mou Fu ship has not been determined. Two Japanese ships, Da Xin and Tenma, are transporting large quantities of Japanese goods and opium for dumping in Likang. The details are as follows:

Shanghai-Wenzhou Shipping Route

Suspended Again

After the Shanghai-Wenzhou route was successfully tested by the British ship New An Lee and returned smoothly to Shanghai, various ships, such as the British ships New Xiang Tai, Shen Fu, and Shen Ai, successively tested the route. However, the Japanese Navy suddenly announced on the evening of the 17th that it would resume the blockade of Wenzhou Bay, causing the route to be blocked and suspended again. The New Xiang Tai of Tai Chang Xiang and the Shen Ai ship of Yi Long Company arrived in Shanghai yesterday with cargo from Wenzhou, but will no longer sail in the future. It is still difficult to predict whether it can reach the destination to load cargo. If the cargo cannot be loaded in time, it will be changed to leave Zhenhai the day after tomorrow.

Large Quantities of Japanese Goods

Dumped in Likang

A reporter from Da Guang News Agency learned from the shipping industry that Likang is a small island in the Zhoushan Islands with a population of over 1,000 households. It is located more than 30 li from the Zhenhai estuary and can be reached by small ferry in one hour. The island has been under the jurisdiction of the Dinghai County Government. Since the fall of Dinghai, the area has been in a state of anarchy, with only 30-odd members of the local self-defense force. The Japanese Navy occasionally lands there, but quickly retreats. Currently, two Japanese ships, Da Xin and Tenma, are sailing back and forth from Shanghai, transporting large quantities of Japanese goods for dumping. The Chinese military and police are unable to exercise their authority there. It is also learned that sailing ships are transporting large quantities of drugs from a certain direction, which are also landing there and then being transshipped elsewhere. Therefore, Likang has become the tail end of Japanese goods and drugs. It is heard that the Ningbo Defense Command is paying close attention to this and prohibits all ships sailing from there to Ningbo from entering the port to prevent Japanese goods and drugs from entering.

Arrested, Tried, and Awaiting Sentence

Chinese constables No. 1663, No. 1228, and No. 2457 of the Gordon Road Police Station were patrolling in the area of Connaught Road and Jessfield Road at 7:15 PM on the 15th of this month when they were suddenly surrounded by a group of about fifteen thugs, each armed with a box cannon, who ordered them to remain silent and robbed them of three handguns and eighteen rounds of ammunition they were carrying.

of Chinese and Western Detectives

flower association lottery factory

Embezzlement of Remittance 76

Both Parties Hold Conflicting Views - Sentencing Scheduled for the 25th

Yuan Xuting, the 33-year-old Ningbo native owner of Yongfeng Rice Store at No. 277 Great Rachel Road, recently hired lawyer Tang Huaiqun to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special No. 2 Court. He accused Hua Shunian (40 years old, from Zhenjiang, currently residing at No. 6, Lane 118, Huanneng Road), who was in charge of business at the Dongtai branch of the Bank of China, of breach of trust and embezzling a remittance of 5,000 yuan. He requested an investigation and also filed a civil suit, requesting a judgment ordering repayment.

Regarding this remittance and the overdue 7% annual interest, the complaint states that on August 21st of the 27th year of the Republic (1938), the plaintiff sent Wei Baoxuan to Taizhou to entrust Jia Xusheng, the business director of the Taixian branch of the Bank of China, to remit 5,000 yuan to Shanghai. At that time, the defendant, Hua Shunian, the business director of the Dongtai branch of the Bank of China, was present and needed the funds for use. Jia Xusheng obtained Wei Baoxuan's consent and handed the funds over to Hua Shunian, who agreed to deliver them in Shanghai on time. The defendant received the funds and issued a formal receipt as proof.

Later, Dongtai fell, and the branch of the Bank of China moved to Shanghai, and the defendant also came to Shanghai to work. For a year now, he has delayed delivering the entrusted remittance of 5,000 yuan. Despite repeated reminders, he has used excuses to delay, and his actions border on embezzlement. The plaintiff requests an investigation and the recovery of the remittance. After receiving the complaint, Judge Sun Pengham conducted a hearing. The defendant requested a postponement to gather evidence, which was granted. These details have been previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, the case was heard again. The plaintiff and his lawyer were present.

They restated the previous situation.

The defendant, Hua Shunian, and his lawyer, E Sen, were present. Hua admitted to receiving the 5,000 yuan from Jia Xusheng but claimed it was part of other transactions. He stated that he had paid two checks totaling 8,000 yuan on February 18th of the previous year. After arriving in Shanghai, he had met with the plaintiff several times to settle accounts, but without success. He also presented the check numbers and account names as evidence. The witness, Wei Baoxuan, was also summoned to testify about the circumstances of the remittance. After hearing the arguments, the court adjourned the hearing and scheduled sentencing for the 25th.

Trends in Teacher Education in Various Countries (1) - Continental European Unified Control Policy 80

(Chongqing Airmail) Professor Qiu Youzheng of a domestic university recently wrote an article entitled "Overview of Teacher Education in Various Countries," in which he elaborates on the trends in teacher education in European, American, Japanese, and Russian countries. Here are some excerpts. We study modern teacher education by referring to seven countries: Germany, France, Italy, England, the United States, Japan, and Russia. There are three trends: (1) Germany, France, and Italy in continental Europe follow a "unified control policy," with extremely strict restrictions on teachers in primary and secondary schools, regarding teacher training colleges as places for teacher certification preparation; (2) England and the United States follow a "laissez-faire system" where educational undertakings are mostly established by non-governmental organizations, local governments, or private individuals, and teacher training is no exception; (3) Japan and Russia, one focusing on the emperor and the other aiming for a communist society, regard teacher training as a tool for implementing national policy, and can therefore be generally termed "instrumentalism." These three approaches have influenced or implied implications for teacher education in China. The evolution of teacher education in China has gone from independence to dependence, and now from dependence to independence. In the early years of the Republic of China, it was roughly modeled after Japan, with national higher normal schools and provincial normal schools, as well as teacher training institutes and vocational teacher training schools. In addition, there were separate women's and men's normal schools of equal standing. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922), a new school system was implemented, and teacher education changed with the six-three-three system. The standards may have been raised, but the spirit of specialized teacher training was implicitly abolished. Provincial normal schools became part of senior high schools, and most national higher normal schools were upgraded to ordinary universities, with only a faculty of education established. This was also a result of the American school system. Currently, Chinese education is stirred by the currents of resistance against Japan and national reconstruction. The education authorities deeply recognize that teachers at all levels of schools bear a great responsibility and that they cannot fulfill their mission without personal, scientific, and specialized training. Therefore, national teacher colleges are being established, and teacher education zones are being planned. Our hope, of course, is to create a system that suits China's actual needs, without simply copying from the East or the West, and to lay a permanent foundation for national role models and moral educators, without the phenomenon of frequent changes. Therefore, how are the current conditions of teacher education in various countries? I think those who are concerned about and study teacher education will want to hear about it. I will now describe the situation in each country below.

Unified Control Policy in Continental Europe

The Jena campaign was the key to the development of teacher education in continental European countries. When Napoleon defeated Prussia, the German philosopher Fichte vehemently called for national awakening, urged the government to quickly seek educational reform, and advocated sending students abroad to study Pestalozzi's educational spirit and methods. Later, these people all became principals of normal schools. By 1825, German teacher education had independent facilities and a solid foundation. France already had achievements in teacher education during the Napoleonic era, but it was not until the Minister of Education Guizot took it under direct state control and required each county to set one up, that the year was 1832. European countries, after this stimulus, all began to engage in operations and regard the training of teachers as one of the special rights of the state. This concept has indeed become a fashion of the times.

(1) France - Primary education in France is the most developed. National elementary schools are required to be set up in each village, regardless of the population, one for boys and one for girls if the population is over 500. Therefore, the training of teachers is also relatively evenly distributed. The current system is based on the decree of 1879, which stipulates that each county should set up one normal school for men and one for women. Therefore, there are currently 88 normal schools for men and women, with only one or two exceptions. The entrance qualification is the level of a general course in a higher elementary school, because the middle school in France has a seven-year course, which is connected to the elementary school. Therefore, the age is 15 to 19 years old. Entrance requires an examination, and there is also an examination at the end of each academic year in the school. In the final academic year, they should practice in their affiliated primary schools. The courses taught include educational psychology, sociology, education, ethics, and philosophy. The decision includes French and literature, history and geography, foreign languages, and teaching. Also, physics and natural history, hygiene, homework, housework, (women) and drawing, sculpture, and geometric drawing, singing, music, and gymnastics are all subjects taught every year. There is also a short time for agricultural theory, and a lot of time for manual work and agriculture, but passing the graduation exam only gets you a high school exemption certificate, and you can serve as an intern educator. After two years of experience, when you are 20 years old, you will be reviewed again. If you pass the test, such as the actual teaching experiment, and the test of education, management, school operation, and practical educational problems, you can get a teacher's certificate of competence, but those who have not fulfilled their military service obligations still do not have this right. Those who obtain this certificate can be employed as full-time teachers. After that, there is still room for free development in the education field.

There are two types of middle schools in France, one is national and the other is locally established. In addition, normal schools and higher primary schools are also in the middle education process. Therefore, there are also two types of teacher training: Higher Normal Schools, one is the secondary higher normal school, the male school is located in Paris, the female school is located in Fossell, and the study period is three or four years. Students are recruited from the two middle schools mentioned above, and they are trained to become teachers in the two middle schools mentioned above. One is the elementary higher normal school, the male school is located in Stcloud, and the female school is located in Fontenayaux roeee. The main body is to recruit graduates of normal schools, the study period is two years, and they are also trained to become teachers in normal schools and higher elementary schools. However, graduates of these two higher normal schools are still test sites in schools. The qualifications are determined by the test. France still cannot immediately obtain the official qualifications of teachers. They still have to go through the test, and the teachers of national middle schools must obtain the title of "Examination and Appointment Professor." The so-called examination and appointment professor must come from the examination. The qualification for the examination is generally those who have a master's degree. Each year, the Ministry of Education calculates the needs of Lycees and holds public examinations. There are eight items: philosophy, literature, grammar, history and geography, foreign languages ​​(English, German, Italian, Spanish, or Arabic), mathematics, physics and chemistry, and even natural history. The so-called secondary higher normal school is of course the standard place for this kind of test.
