Free Talk

Not Defending Critics 91

— Chen Xi

The transformations in the literary world are truly numerous. There was a period when critics specialized in criticizing writers. Later, writers joined forces with non-writers to criticize the critics. Until recently, this situation has become less heated.

The underlying reason is roughly this: Some writers, due to the "slander" of critics (whether it is "slander" or "setting up slander" is still a question), although living in such a great era, ended up withdrawing their literary works and waiting, waiting for an opportunity for critics to also produce creative works, so they could also criticize. If they waited long without seeing any works, they would also scold: "You say this article is not good, this article is too bad, but you yourself can't write a single good piece for people to read!" Critics seemed to understand this point, so they only shouted "no works," and they were determined to be scolded by writers and "never produce anything." Writers had no choice but to sigh and walk away.

Truthfully speaking, unless a writer's work is "hidden in famous mountains to be passed down to future generations," then he alone can appreciate it himself, or boast about it himself. People (readers and critics) will definitely not say "not good" or "too bad," and even if they want to say it, there's no way to say it. But the era of "hiding in famous mountains" has long passed, and they also feel that they are eating animals, and they cannot starve themselves and sing high-sounding praises all day long. So they can only put their works into society. Once they enter society, they have value, which is a commodity, and immediately become "copyrighted." If someone is willing to offer a price to buy it, then they have at least paid a price, and they seem to have the right to say good or bad. In this way, "criticism" is truly a sin that writers should endure. In fact, if writing a work is said to be "unpleasant" because it has been criticized a few times, it is a bit too much. I think that being criticized is not without benefit to the writer. Saying it's good can make the work spread more widely, and saying it's bad can also let the author know their shortcomings, as long as the critic is honest (without bias) and the author is humble!

Of course, writers resent critics partly because critics sit high in the literary world and look down on everything, leading to situations of random criticism and slander. But this should not lead to throwing out the baby with the bathwater, and the essence of criticism should not be erased because of this one point. Moreover, in my opinion, incorrect "random criticism" cannot be "immortal," and someone will definitely refute it soon. But now, some writers have withdrawn their works because of the criticism of critics, with the intention of leaving the literary world blank. However, such silence and inactivity are not beneficial to the literary world!

The criticism of critics is considered "slander" by writers, but third parties may think it is the most appropriate judgment. The problem is that writers should not take "my own writing is the best" as the ultimate truth, because critics cannot falsely point to a prostitute and say, "She is the greatest hero in the world!" just because the writer is someone they know and want to get some good from them. Nor can they call a real hero a prostitute because of their dislike for the author.

As for writers putting down their pens and waiting for the critics' works, this is almost a joke. People have already used the analogy of cooks and diners, so I will skip it here.

I am not a critic, there is no need to defend critics, and there is no possibility of resenting creators. If I must state my position, then the above words are all the opinions of an ordinary reader.

Squad Leader 92

— Ding Shan

Long and sturdy, his chest was like a piece of iron, so hard and stiff, his face was covered with small red bumps. Not very lively, but extremely energetic, his eyes always stared at people's faces - I almost blushed from their gaze several times.

This was my squad leader during training, an eleventh-term recruit at the military academy.

He was fierce and unreasonable. When he glared and roared, "There is no reason in the army. If there is reason, the order is the reason!" we were frightened and hung our heads, because if we had a slightly unpleasant expression, his long legs would sweep over, which would make you hurt for a whole day.

Perhaps he had not forgotten that we were ultimately from "young master" backgrounds, (as he said) when we were doing hard field exercises, everyone showed a helpless expression and kept pulling at their grass-green wide sleeves to wipe sweat. He would say like an older brother, half mocking, half pitifully: "Look! How useless! When you go to the battlefield and 'lie down', you won't be able to get up! I'm telling you, sweat more in the training ground, bleed less on the battlefield... Hmph, take a break - about face, you should also release your 'water guns'."

He really liked to joke. When he was free, he would chat with us about everything, and he loved to ask if we had lovers. We asked him the same question, and he would smile happily and say: "Yes! Her name is Jin Cang - we will get married when the time comes, and I will have to hug her and sleep on the battlefield at night!"

The squad leader was from Jilin. When asked about "home," his jaw dropped a little, but he immediately raised it higher, and his not-so-lively pupils became more fixed, and his chest became straighter. Apart from the dry words "Changchun," he didn't say anything else. At other times, when he was happy, he would tell himself that he had done unprofitable business on Xiaobai Mountain (he smiled when he said it), and he had been taught by ghosts (he sneered when he said it)...

"For justice, for survival, for freedom, war should not be avoided." When we disbanded in August of last year, he said excitedly, "My wish to enter military academy can also be fulfilled."

"Will we ever see each other again?" I asked mournfully inexplicably.

"Why not?" he roared. "In Jilin!"

"I'm not from Jilin!"

"You are Chinese," he looked at me warmly and smiled lightly. - I really can't forget that bright smile.

In the past two years, he and his lover must have already gotten married, and they must have a "child," fulfilling the squad leader's wish of "marriage," I thought.

Are the Germans Really Not Afraid of Defeat? (Part 2) 93

— Written by Fritz Sternberg, Translated by Zhu Jijun

Geographically speaking, France may achieve a brilliant victory in this war, but at the same time, many people in Germany also believe (as they did in 1914) that they can achieve a superior victory within a few months. However, in the West, Germany is facing a country whose industrial level is also very high (although in some production sectors, it is behind Germany). It can technically, chemically, mechanically, in the air, and with poison gas, contend with Germany. Therefore, it is impossible for Germany to calmly achieve a military victory in the West. Thus, in the West, there are neither industrial nor military conditions that can enable Germany to achieve a brilliant victory. In the East, there are even fewer of these two good conditions, and even the geographical conditions are lacking.

Therefore, judging from a purely military point of view, the Second World War will be a long-term war - unless the masses of the people come out to stop it. A long-term war is the greatest danger to Germany's National Socialist rule, because as the war drags on, those factors that gave Germany some military advantages in the early stages of the war (the mobilization of the entire military industry) will, in turn, poison it.

If Germany had used its productivity to the fullest when the war started, then later it would not be able to increase its production significantly, because it would soon reach its peak, and thereafter, productivity would begin to decline, and would decline sharply at an unprecedented rate.

On the other hand, if a country has a very outstanding peacetime productivity in the years before the outbreak of the war, even in the years of military expansion, then it still has a lot of room to work hard during the war, and greatly increase the productivity of its military industry. At the same time, the peak of productivity can be reached later, and the rate of its decline can also be slightly slower. However, Germany is not like this.

Unless German fascism wins quickly, it will not be able to win at all, because due to the long-term development of anti-government tendencies in Germany, the rate of productivity decline (which will come as the war drags on) will increase dramatically. The Second World War will be a long-term war, and National Socialist Germany will not wait for the end of the war and will be reduced first.

When Hohenzollern Germany plunged into the whirlpool of the Great War, it was only prepared militarily and did not plan economically in advance. It had economic weaknesses and was defeated. The Allied countries won because of their superiority in steel, iron, and food.

Fascist Germany is seeking lessons from the Great War. It is simultaneously building a military and an economic general staff to plunge into the vortex of the Second World War, and it will simultaneously plunge into the vortex as a fascist country. Only that.

However, merely having a military and economic general staff cannot win a war. The support of the masses of the people is also necessary. But now, most of them oppose National Socialist rule, although this opposition is latent and secret.

If the war drags on for a long time, then Himmler's prediction, that in this Second World War, a civil war will inevitably occur in Germany, will be terribly fulfilled.

How long can Hitler support the war?

Only enough to support a fierce war.

But not long enough for the long period required by the Second World War.

What Counts -- One's Own Fate! 94

— Bi Ying

At this time,

In this situation,

What counts --

One's own fate!

No need for decadent music,

No need for moaning without illness,

Only anger and furious flames,

Burning the bloody soul,

Ringing out loudly.

I want to run --

Towards those distant mountains and ridges,

To leap,

To lurk,

Give play to the instinct of justice,

I do not wish

In a narrow world,

To shrink and survive.

The distant base camp,

Is the soul of the nation,

I will go there,

To love and be intimate with it.

Run!

What counts --

One's own fate!

The Entertainment World

After a Thousand Calls, She Finally Appears: Song Dezhu to Perform on Stage the Day After Tomorrow 96

— Wei Wei

Nan Tiesheng stopped performing "Golden Shackles" yesterday (the 18th). After Tiesheng finished performing, the authorities of the Golden Theater originally intended to invite the female performer Zhang Eyun to take the stage next, to perform for a few days, while waiting for Song Dezhu and other Peking opera performers from Xiao Kelaishen, who had been invited long ago but were blocked by the floods, to arrive, and then give up the stage. Now, since Song Dezhu and his party arrived in Shanghai a few days ago (the 17th) on the Shuntian Wheel, Zhang Eyun's plan to perform at the Golden Theater after Nan Tiesheng has become a pipe dream.

This time, the Golden Theater invited Song Dezhu, Yang Baosen, Wu Yanheng, and other large groups of Peking opera performers. I have introduced them one by one in this newspaper. Now, it is known that in addition to the people who were invited before, Yuan Shihai and Ci Shaoquan have also joined and came with Song Yang and others.

Yuan Shihai once came to Shanghai with Shang Xiaoyun, but he failed to leave a deep impression on the people of Shanghai. In fact, Shihai's art is worth mentioning. Shihai specializes in the painted-face roles in Peking opera, and he is an outstanding talent from the fifth class of Fu Liancheng. During his time in the class, he secretly studied with his eldest brother, Hou Xirui. All of Hou's masterpieces, such as "Ding Zishan at the Famen Temple," "Mu Kezhai," "Puqiu Mountain," and "Stealing the Imperial Horse," are all Shihai's specialties. After leaving the class, he was invited by famous actors such as Shang Xiaoyun and Xiao Cuihua, and his art was further developed by secretly imitating Hao Shoushen after Hou Xirui. Shoushen was known as the "Living Cao Cao" in the old capital, because Shoushen's performance of Cao Cao was so realistic. Shihai's white-faced plays are modeled after Shoushen. Over time, he has also become full of Hao's style. All of Hao's masterpieces, such as "Huang Yidao," "Peach Blossom Village," and "The Trial of Li Qi," are well-received by Shihai. Recently, Shihai has even joined Shoushen's school and become Hao's disciple. Shihai's voice is not very powerful, but his rhyme is full. His stage presence can be said to be beautiful. Although he has joined Hao's school, his art is actually close to Hou's, and Shihai learned a lot from Hou when he was in the class. I think that Shihai should take the essence of Hou and Hao and combine them into one. With Shihai's talent and good foundation, his future is unlimited if he can do so. Ci Shaoquan is the son of the famous comedian Ci Ruiquan. He has followed Cheng Yanqiu south several times. His acting is conventional, neither greasy nor slippery. He has the style of his father, but Shaoquan has never been popular and has always been in the position of a supporting actor. This time, he is going south, and perhaps he can show his talents.

Song Dezhu, Yang Baosen, and others are scheduled to take the stage at the Golden Theater starting on the 21st. Song Dezhu's three-day performance schedule has been slightly changed from the previous one. The first day will be the complete "Xin'an Post Station," which is a secret book of the old Narcissus Flower, which is different from the one performed by Mao Shilai before. The second day is "Water Flooding Jinshan Temple," which is Dezhu's masterpiece. Huang Liushuang invited Dezhu to shoot this play into a film and take it to the United States for screening. The third day is "The Great Heroine." Since Song Dezhu left the opera school, she has shown her sharp edge. Her popularity in Beijing is not inferior to that of the famous Western dan. This is her first time going south, and it is difficult to predict whether she can appeal to the audience. However, Song and his party are mostly excellent talents from the opera school and Fu Liancheng. Although they are young talents, they are all rising stars, and it is expected that they will give the people of Shanghai a new look.

The Two Major State-Run Film Studios in Chongqing Have No Worries About Film Stock 97

— Hui Cun

Filming work is not affected

Since the outbreak of the Second European War, the source of film stock has been greatly affected, because the products of the German Agfa factory are in danger of being cut off. Although there are still a few stocks currently, the ships of the warring countries have been transferred back to their countries for military use, so many difficulties have occurred in transportation, and the price has also risen several times.

Currently, the largest supplier of film stock is Kodak of the United States. Because the United States has not yet been involved in the whirlpool of war, it continues to produce in large quantities to meet the needs of the film industry in various countries.

In the past, the two major state-run film studios in Chongqing, "China" and "China Electric," have always felt that the source of film stock was not easy to obtain. Before the outbreak of the European War, transportation was already quite difficult, and the days were often delayed due to avoiding air raids, which affected filming work. After the outbreak of the European War, the outside world speculated that the source of film stock would be even more difficult. If the United States joined the war, the Kodak company would have no products to meet the needs, so not only "China Electric" and "China" would have no films to shoot, but also the film industry in various countries would be greatly affected. However, in fact, "China Electric" and "China" had already planned ahead. Currently, the Hong Kong factory of "China" has purchased and stored a large amount of film stock, and "China Electric" also sent photography director Zhou Ke to Hong Kong not long ago to negotiate on film stock matters, and he has also purchased a lot and temporarily stored it in Hong Kong. As soon as it is needed, it can be transported to Chongqing at any time. Therefore, at present, even if the products of Kodak in the United States are cut off, the film stock of the two major state-run film studios in Chongqing can still be said to be safe in the short term.

Indian sensual star Sarbo and newcomer John Justing in the dadga fOfeihTehT look very carefree.

Young Musician Chen Gexin (Part 1) 98

— Tianma

- To Answer Questions for the New Capital

The young musician Chen Gexin has been in Shanghai for almost ten years, but he is still only twenty-six years old. He is so young, especially his youthfulness in the spirit of struggling for music. Gexin himself is very capable of writing articles. In the past, he has published many light and sharp essays in various newspapers. He does not have a very good background. He has gradually come to understand music through his own hard work and intelligence. Moreover, he is proficient in English, French, Russian, and other languages.

As for his family, his wife Jin Jiaoli is also a beautiful girl who can sing Western tunes. He has always been so indifferent. None of his friends have ever heard him say that Chen Bai, who was once popular in the Shanghai education circle, is his own brother, but the brothers have completely different interests and personalities.

He can compose, write lyrics, and play musical instruments. His songs, works, and performances are already familiar to readers in various films, theaters, and newspapers. And now, he is in charge of the "orchestra" and "song and dance group" of the "new song and dance" at the "New Capital Hotel" of the New New Company.

Liu Qiong and Xia Xia Collaborate for the First Time 100

— Beni

"The Beginning of Man" was performed by the "Shanghai Drama Society" at the Grand Auditorium of the French Municipal Council last year. Due to the original author Ba Ruolai's bloody satire and delicate portrayal, it caused a sensation in the drama world after the performance. Later, Xinhua Company planned to film "The Beginning of Man." After several negotiations, it was finally successful. At that time, it was decided that Liu Qiong would play the male role (Zhang Bonan) and Gu Lanjun would play the female lead (Xiao Lilian). The film was named "The World of Gold and Silver" and was well received by the famous world after its release.

Recently, the "Shanghai Drama Society" has been performing at the "Xuan Palace Theater" for a long time. It was originally planned to re-enact "The Beginning of Man" with the original cast around the Mid-Autumn Festival, which was a month ago.

Later, it was said that Gu Degang, who originally played Zhang Bonan, could not perform due to circumstances, and Shu Shi? "Sunrise" is being performed vigorously, so he naturally cannot spare himself. In this way, the authorities of the Drama Society considered new candidates. At this time, Wu Yonggang, who was just in "Flowers Splashing Tears," was often in the Drama Society (because he was the director of "Flowers Splashing Tears"). So, after everyone discussed together, they thought of Liu Qiong in "The World of Gold and Silver." After discussion, there was no problem. As for the role originally played by Shu Shi, it will be played by Mao Yun, who played Zhao Shengzhai in "Shen Yuan." This is also a "well-deserved" arrangement.

This is the first time that Xia Xia and Liu Qiong have collaborated on the stage. Under the direction of the "exquisite and detailed" director Mr. Wu Renzhi, the performance results will probably be correct.
